This hotel is the only Shangri-La brand hotel in China with hot springs. The biggest feature is the seawater hot spring. The hot spring pool can be selected from 38 degrees to 41 degrees. The hot spring water quality is great and the hygiene is in place, maintaining the standards of the Shangri-La brand. The hotel service staff is warm and thoughtful, and the room linens are also very comfortable. I like the design of the bathroom, which takes into account the needs of girls' cosmetics display tables, and the details are great. I recommend Shangri-La for vacation in Putian. Compared with Shangri-La hotels in other cities, Putian has a very high cost performance.

The lobby decoration is exquisite There are Fujian style and a little Japanese style, the overall hardware design is very careful and meticulous, the room is small, low-key luxury, decorated with a lot of wood grain, the service staff is very good, not the enthusiasm from the show kind, but they all answered my questions patiently with a shy expression, which is great.
There are not many types of breakfast, but the presentation is exquisite and thoughtful, the taste is also very good, the dining environment is also very comfortable, the gym facilities are very complete, the swimming pool is very clean and there are very few people.
Although the hotel is a bit far from the city center, it is a good deal to spend an extra 20 yuan for an online car-hailing car to go to Xinghua Prefecture.
Although they are all very good, I still have to complain about two things. When I checked in, I told that I needed to add Shangri-La membership points. The supervisor at the counter told me that I couldnâ€™t have points because I booked with Ctrip. I didnâ€™t understand. In addition, many people said in the comments that the hotel will upgrade the room to a lake-view room. I saw that there were very few guests staying in the hotel that day. I may be sorry for my long face. The floor given to me was very low and faced the main road. In most five-star hotels, if there are not many guests, I will arrange an upgrade, not to mention that I am a member of them and a diamond member of Ctrip. I was upgraded at the InterContinental in Fuzhou the day before.
One last thing, Ctrip told me that the check-out time is 2:00 pm, and there was a piece of paper in the room card that said check-out was at 12:00 noon, so I asked her, and the system only said yes after checking.

msg:The hotel has a good view, you can see the Shouxi River, and there is also a small road directly into the Shouxi Park. The room facilities are new, the area is large, the dry and wet are separated, and there are double sinks. I just went in and didn't find the charging port, it was hidden in the drawer, and Wireless fast charging, very convenient. There is also a small square table in the room, suitable for working and dining. What is commendable is the sanitation of the hotel, which is very clean and tidy, and the family members who are obsessed with cleanliness are very satisfied! There are many types of breakfast, Chinese style, as well as flat food and meatballs similar to soy meat, you can experience Putian cuisine without going out. The hotel has sufficient parking spaces for self-driving travel. The staff has a good service attitude, especially last night when I walked to the door of the room with a takeaway, I couldn't get my room card to open the door. The staff brother who happened to pass by rushed forward and took the initiative to help with the things, thank you!
